      "Layered gold necklaces"
    ],

{
  "subject": "a very beautiful young woman taking a close-up selfie",
  "age": "19-22 years old",
  "ethnicity": "East Asian with slight Western mix, fair porcelain skin",
  "face": "perfect symmetrical heart-shaped face, small straight nose, high cheekbones, soft jawline, flawless smooth skin with no blemishes",
  "eyes": "large almond-shaped doe eyes, dark brown irises, long thick natural eyelashes, sharp winged eyeliner, subtle smoky lower eyeliner",
  "eyebrows": "thick straight Korean-style brows, perfectly groomed and filled",
  "makeup": "dewy glowing skin, soft pink blush on cheeks, matte rosy-nude lipstick, slight lip overlining for pouty look, subtle highlight on nose bridge and cupid's bow",
  "lips": "full pouty lips in a slight duck-face expression",
  "hair": "jet-black straight hair, shoulder-length with soft layers, center-parted, slightly messy front strands framing the face, glossy and healthy",
  "pose": "selfie taken with phone in right hand (arm visible at bottom right), head slightly tilted, looking directly at camera with soft seductive expression",
  "hand_gesture": "left hand raised doing a small peace sign (V sign) near her face, long clear acrylic nails with natural french tips",
  "clothing": "vintage black band T-shirt, slightly cropped/fitted, yellow and black graphic print on chest with distorted '{argument name="band name" default="ROADRUNNER"}' text in bold retro font and faded band photo underneath, soft worn cotton texture",
  "accessories": "large thin silver hoop earrings, oversized black rectangular sunglasses resting on top of her head",
  "background": "modern minimalist indoor setting, soft natural daylight, blurred white walls and ceiling, hint of a kitchen or hallway in the background",
  "lighting": "soft diffused natural window light from the front-left, gentle shadows, bright but not harsh, slight glow on skin",
  "camera": "front-facing smartphone camera, slight wide-angle selfie distortion, high resolution, sharp focus on face",
  "aesthetic": "Korean/Chinese ulzzang + douyin + soft e-girl, clean beauty, 2020s Instagram influencer vibe",
  "mood": "cute but slightly edgy, playful, confident, effortlessly cool",
  "quality_tags": "ultra-detailed, photorealistic, 8k, sharp focus, beautiful lighting, cinematic, highly detailed skin texture, realistic eyes reflection",
  "negative_prompt": "blurry, deformed, extra limbs, bad anatomy, overexposed, plastic skin, doll-like, text artifacts, watermark, logo"

### 19. Nano Banana Pro 的 Vlog 风格视频拍摄提示（Veo 3.1 的图像输入）

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-16  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成图像，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 将其转换为视频。该提示描述了一个逼真、亲密的 vlog 风格镜头，一名女性正在谈论她的时尚，重点关注构图、光线和氛围。此提示用于图像生成步骤 (Nano Banana Pro)。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは{argument name="ファッションの特徴" default="【ファッションの特徴を追加】"}がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

### 23. Vlog 风格视频生成提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-13  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一位女性使用 Nano Banana Pro (Gemini 3 Pro Image) 的视频风格镜头，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 进行动画处理。该提示侧重于逼真的光线、构图和适合时尚视频博客的自然、放松的表情。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

The composition feels spontaneous and personal, like a late-night moment captured on film. The lighting is soft and direct, reminiscent of on-camera flash photography, creating gentle highlights on skin and fabric while preserving natural imperfections. White bedding fills most of the frame, keeping the focus on the subjects and their quiet connection. The mood is warm, intimate, and authentic—more emotional than posed.

Style & Quality Cues
Photorealistic, candid lifestyle photography, film-camera aesthetic, subtle grain, natural skin texture, raw and intimate mood

Lighting
Soft direct flash, low ambient light, gentle shadows, realistic contrast

Camera
Close-range portrait shot, eye-level angle, shallow depth of field, 35mm film look

Aspect Ratio
3:4

Negative Prompt
, exaggerated anatomy, glamour lighting, studio setup, over-smoothed skin, cartoon style, AI artifacts, harsh color grading
```

[[Natural Skin Texture]] [[Direct Flash]]

### 67. 一位女性吃披萨的超逼真抓拍闪光肖像

### 69. 3x3 逼真美妆摄影网格，带身份锁定

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2025-12-23  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的提示，旨在生成一个 3x3 的逼真图像网格，其中包含同一位女性（严格锁定身份），在干净的摄影棚环境中进行各种“准备”动作。它要求所有九个图块在光线、背景和身份上保持一致，并专注于自然的皮肤纹理和美妆道具。

![3x3 逼真美妆摄影网格，带身份锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766673207018_mpzdds_G83vlRDWoAA-Eri.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid",
      "version": "v1.0",
      "priority": "high"
    },
    "references": {
      "character_reference_image": "UPLOAD_YOUR_CHARACTER_REFERENCE (FACE OR FULLBODY)",
      "style_reference_image": "OPTIONAL_UPLOAD_THIS_3x3_COLLAGE_AS_STYLE/ACTION_REF",
      "reference_rules": {
        "preserve_uploaded_character_identity": true,
        "identity_lock_strength": 0.98,
        "use_style_reference_for": ["set", "wardrobe", "lighting", "actions"],
        "do_not_copy_style_reference_identity": true
      }
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "layout": {
        "type": "3x3_grid",
        "border": "thin_white_gutter",
        "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_room_same_lighting"
      },
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "photorealistic_editorial",
      "sharpness": "high",
      "film_grain": "subtle"
    },
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Create a 3x3 photoreal studio grid showing the SAME woman (strict identity lock) in a clean beauty-bathroom photoshoot vibe. Same neutral light-gray/white seamless background, same camera distance, same lighting. Wardrobe: white bathrobe throughout. Prop continuity: towel, tiara/crown, lipstick, hairbrush, comb, toothbrush, face mask, cucumber slices. Each tile shows a different playful 'getting ready' moment. Keep faces fully visible in every tile.",
      "global_rules": {
        "same_person": "MUST_MATCH_CHARACTER_REFERENCE (face/skin tone/eyes/nose/mouth proportions)",
        "same_lighting": "soft studio key light + gentle fill; consistent shadows across tiles",
        "same_camera": "full-frame DSLR look, 50mm or 85mm; same framing and distance",
        "background": "plain seamless studio backdrop, no clutter, no extra people",
        "skin_texture": "natural pores, no plastic smoothing"
      },
      "tiles": [
        {
          "tile_id": 1,
          "action": "Towel wrapped as a turban; woman adjusting the towel with one hand near forehead; playful surprised expression."
        },
        {
          "tile_id": 2,
          "action": "Hair down; singing into a hairbrush like a microphone; eyes closed or dramatic singing face; energetic."
        },
        {
          "tile_id": 3,
          "action": "Putting a sparkling tiara/crown on her head with both hands; focused, slightly serious expression."
        },
        {
          "tile_id": 4,

        },
        {

        },

### 75. 伦勃朗布光下的超写实餐厅肖像

**Author**: [Harshith](https://x.com/HarshithLucky3)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 这是一个详细的、超现实的图像生成提示，用于比较 Nano Banana Pro 和 GPT Image 1.5。它描述了一位年轻女性在一家高档、光线昏暗的餐厅中的半身肖像，强调电影般的暖光（伦勃朗布光）、自然的皮肤纹理以及特定的相机设置（索尼 A7R IV，85mm f/1.2 GM 镜头），以呈现原始摄影风格。

### 89. 赛博工业碳纤维物体变形

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示模板，旨在将任何输入对象（例如，老虎、骷髅、运动鞋）转换为复杂、高性能的赛博工业装配。它指定了材料替换（碳纤维、炮铜聚合物）、内部机械结构（布线、霓虹光效）和技术渲染细节（硬表面建模、等距 3D 渲染）。

```
<instructions> 

Input Variable: {argument name="object" default="[INSERT OBJECT]"} (e.g., A Sneaker, A Human Skull, A Cheeseburger, The Letter 'A')

System Instruction:
Reimagine the Input Object as a complex, high-performance Cyber-Industrial Assembly.
 If person or animal, preserve the exact pose, camera anlge, made the hair or fur out of carbon fiber or appropriate material.

1. The "Chassis" Deconstruction:
   The Shell: Replace the object's natural skin with Matte Black Carbon Fiber and Gunmetal Grey Polymer.
   The Segmentation: The object is not solid. It is segmented into distinct panels (like Iron Man armor or a high-end camera body), held together by visible Hex Bolts and Rivets.
   The Gaps: Between the panels, leave small gaps to reveal the internal mechanics.

2. The "Vein" System (Internal Mechanics):
   The Piping: Where organic veins or structure would be, insert Bundled Industrial Cabling and Braided Steel Hoses.
   The Flow: These cables must look functional, routing power from a central core to the extremities of the object.
   The Glow (The Soul):
       Color: Identify the "Spirit Color" of the object (e.g., Burger = Amber/Orange; Skull = Cyan/Blue; Sneaker = Neon Green).
       Source: Hidden LED strips and neon tubes run parallel to the cables, casting a strong internal glow that spills out from the panel gaps.

3. The Narrative Micro-Detail (The Greebles):
   Scale Indicators: Embed tiny technical details to sell the scale.
       Vents: Cooling fans or intake grilles.
       Text: Tiny white serial numbers and warning labels (e.g., "CAUTION: HOT", "NO STEP") printed on the casing.
       The "City" (Optional): If the object is large enough, tiny architectural elements (antennas, platforms) can grow out of the mechanical base.

4. Visual Syntax & Composition:
   Background: Clean Studio Grey (Infinite Curve). The focus is entirely on the object's silhouette.
   Lighting:
       Key Light: Soft white studio light to highlight the texture of the carbon fiber weave.
       Rim Light: A sharp backlight to define the edge of the object against the grey background.
       Bloom: The internal colored LEDs must have a soft "Octane Bloom" effect.

5. Render Style:
   Aesthetic: Hard Surface Modeling, "Tech-Wear" Fashion, High-End Automotive Design.
   Camera: Isometric or 3/4 Product Shot angle.

Output: Photorealistic 3D Render, 8k, Highly Detailed Textures (Carbon Fiber, Brushed Metal, Rubber).
</instructions>
```

[[Neon Lighting]] [[Industrial Design]]

Hard directional daylight as the only light source. High contrast with deep, dense shadows on the facial structure and folds of clothing. No fill light.

### 126. 2x2 Grid Influencer Photoshoot in Private Jet Prompt

**Author**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art)  **Date**: 2025-12-23  **Language**: en

> A complex JSON prompt structure for generating a 2x2 multi-panel grid of photorealistic reference images of an influencer inside a luxurious private jet, ensuring character consistency across all frames and defining specific poses and expressions.

![2x2 Grid Influencer Photoshoot in Private Jet Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766673086960_g0h64e_G8p_aaCW8AAv8H2.jpg)

```
{
    "generation_request": {
      "meta_data": { "tool": "NanoBananaPro", "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid", "version": "v1.0" },
      "output_settings": { "layout": { "type": "2x2_grid", "border": "thin_white_gutter", "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_outfit" }, "aspect_ratio": "4:5", "resolution": "ultra_high_res", "render_style": "luxurious_warm_interior" },
      "reference_constraints": { "character_reference_image": "UPLOAD_REF_IMAGE", "use_reference_face_only": true, "identity_lock": true, "strict_face_match": true },
      "global_prompt": {
        "scene": "Interior of a Gulfstream Private Jet. Cream leather seats, mahogany wood tables. View of clouds through oval windows.",
        "subject": {
          "type": "influencer",
          "identity": "same person as reference image",
          "hair": "loose blowout, expensive highlights",
          "makeup": "matte flawless base, nude lip",
          "outfit": "cashmere lounge set in beige, slide sandals, diamond studs",
          "prop": "champagne flute or magazines"
        },
        "camera": { "capture": "rich lifestyle", "lens_equivalent": "35mm", "focus": "subject", "depth_of_field": "sharp" }
      },
      "frames": [
        { "frame_id": "A", "position": "top_left", "shot_type": "looking_out_window", "pose": "Looking out the window dreamily, holding champagne.", "expression": "thoughtful, rich" },
        { "frame_id": "B", "position": "top_right", "shot_type": "reading_mag", "pose": "Legs curled up on the seat, reading a vogue magazine.", "expression": "relaxed" },
        { "frame_id": "C", "position": "bottom_left", "shot_type": "cheers_camera", "pose": "Toasting the camera with the glass, big smile.", "expression": "celebratory" },
        { "frame_id": "D", "position": "bottom_right", "shot_type": "sleeping_mask", "pose": "Fake sleeping with a silk eye mask pushed up on forehead.", "expression": "peaceful" }
      ]
    }
  }
```

(Texture & Quality - CRITICAL):

The figure looks like a tangible, expensive collector's item (Good Smile Company or Alter quality).
A clear acrylic circular base supports the figure.

(Background: 3D Workspace):
Behind the figure, a computer monitor displays a (3D modeling software interface:1.5) (like Blender, Maya, or ZBrush).
On the screen: A (grey wireframe mesh or untextured clay render:1.5) of the SAME character is visible.
The screen represents the digital prototype of the physical figure.

(Surroundings):
The figure's retail packaging box stands vertically next to the figure, featuring the character art.
A blurred mechanical keyboard and mouse are visible in the background.
Soft, professional studio lighting illuminates the figure from above.

(Technical Tags): (depth of field:1.4), (bokeh:1.3), (PVC texture:1.5), (figure photography:1.4), (ray tracing), sharp focus on figure face.
(Negative prompt): (2D illustration:1.6), (anime style:1.5), (drawing), (sketch), (distorted face:1.5), (melted plastic), (bad painting), (messy desk), (screen off), (wrong character on screen), low quality, blurry.
